The idea was to find a winner amongst these 3, and then further extend the competition.\n\nBefore leaving home (G.Jauhar) I ordered MYOB and asked for their Mushroom Madness, which I was to pick from Boat Basin, since that is their only take-away spot. I reached the decided spot about 10 minutes before the MYOB-rider was to show up. He reached the place on time, and to do justice, I had decided earlier to eat the burger the instant I receive it, just to remove any ambiguities of it getting cold/stale etc. Mushroom Madness was a decent enough burger. I had major issues with it's bun, which made it's duty to annoy me till the very end. The bun kept on breaking and crumbling, and the sauces made it extremely soggy; more like a wet-dipped bread. The burger itself was nice enough, in terms of taste.\n\nNext up was The Burger Factory. My intentions were to try the mushroom-topped burgers of the 3 joints, but knowing that TBF doesn't have one, I opted for Ironman Double. It was again a nice burger, eaten as soon as it was served. The amount of cheese did justice to it's description, and the patty was comparatively MUCH softer than the MYOB patty. The MYOB patty was a bit firm. So till now, MYOB vs. TBF and TBF won.\n\nAnd finally, the last stop (after having a Hazelnut Cappuccino from Espresso) was The Burger Shack. Ordered the Shack Shroom Double, and yes there was a small queue (TBF was deserted). Received the order in 17 minutes or so. Closed my eyes, dug in for the first bite.\n*swoosh*\nI was in an entirely different landscape. With soft buns floating around me, the right amount of mushroom topping, not making the bun go soggy and a pain to deal with. And then my palates detected the first hint of the TBS-beef. Sold. Absolutely sold all over again. I was a TBS-loyal ever since I first had it, but when going out on today's expedition, my aim was to give every place a fair chance, and not be biased. I opened my eyes and the reason for the queue outside TBS everytime I went there was answered by the bite of Shack Shroom in my mouth.\n\nMYOB vs. TBF vs. TBS\nHands down, of these three, The Burger Shack is the winner.\nMy next venture would be to compare The Burger Shack and Burger Inc.\n\nEat on After reading and hearing rather polarised opinions about MYOB, the wife and I decided that a tasting shall put many questions to rest and put the mind (and stomach) at ease. We ordered the Combo 2, which brings you the Half Pounder, Onion Rings, Belgian Fries and a Drink. Onion rings were out of stock, so we got the Mozzarella sticks instead, which is where things started to go wrong. The coating was fine, it was nice and somewhat crispy, but the mozzarella inside was rubber. Not cool. The Belgian Fries were fries alright, but we missed the whole Belgian point. They were regular fries, and fairly standard ones at that. But onto the main star of the evening, the famous half pounder. The intensity of the unwrapping of the burger was comparable to the unveiling of a new iPhone. The suspense rivalled that of any good episode of the Zee Horror Show (anyone still remember that?). And when the burger was finally revealed, the big, juicy looking patties, sandwiched in cheese and mayo looked very, very promising indeed. Could it be that we had finally met the burger that deserves to be united with man in holy matrimony? The answer was but a bite away. Now, at this point, I would love to say that with that first bite, the world slowed down, an orchestra struck up a slowly swelling concerto of violin notes and the gates of culinary heaven opened slowly. But none of this happened. Supreme disappointment reined. I took a second bite, convinced that my taste buds had lost all control of their senses. And then a third bite. And a fourth. Einstein once said that doing the same thing over and over again and expecting different results is stupidity - and it was. The glorious half pounder, the burger that promised so much, delivered so little. It was big and very very filling, I'll say that. But it lacked flavour, it lacked that special something that makes you say 'oh dear lord'. It didn't give me the same kind of tingly feeling I had when I first tried Burger Shack or even the somewhat BurgerKingy feeling that I get when I have a double patty original from FatBurger. It was just another burger, and sadly, one that did not climb very high on my top ten burger list. I would say that Burger Shack, FatBurger and even Mr Burger are certainly better in terms of taste and flavour. The patty was very well cooked, nice and even, the burger was well assembled and well preserved in the packaging. All of this is great, but if it doesn't taste as good as it looks, its like getting into a Ferrari and finding out it runs on CNG.","type":"status","created_time":"2013-07-22T19:47:51+0000","updated_time":"2013-07-24T10:44:04+0000","likes":{"data":[{"id":"1443166426","name":"Surayya Amin"},{"id":"509686069","name":"Hasaan
